**GT:** `0.7391218893246799*A**2/(0.8913296033617462*A**4 + 1) - 0.3009370469546767*A*exp(-0.06776739623123975*t)`

The GT has two terms:
1. A rational function: `k1 * A^2 / (k2 * A^4 + 1)` — this is NOT a polynomial in A; it's a rational function with A^4 in the denominator.
2. An exponential decay in t multiplied by A: `k3 * A * exp(k4 * t)`

Key structural features:
- The rational term `A^2/(c*A^4+1)` cannot be expressed as a polynomial in A, nor as `A^2 + terms/A^5`, nor as simple fractions like `A/(A+c)`.
- The exponential term is `A * exp(c*t)` (linear in A, exponential in t).

Let me check each candidate systematically. I'll focus on whether each candidate can produce the rational function `A^2/(c*A^4+1)` and the term `A*exp(c*t)`.

**Key analysis for the rational term:** `A^2/(c*A^4+1)` — For large A, this behaves like `1/(c*A^2)`, and for small A, like `A^2`. No polynomial or polynomial + 1/A^5 can replicate this. The term `A^c/(A^c + d)` with appropriate c can match if structured correctly.

Let me check candidates with `A**c/(A**c + d)` type terms:

**Candidate 3:** Has `A**c5*c6/(A**c5 + c7)`. Setting c5=2: `c6*A^2/(A^2+c7)`. But GT needs `A^2/(c*A^4+1)`. These are different rational functions — `A^2/(A^2+c)` vs `A^2/(c*A^4+1)`. Not equivalent.

Wait, but c5 is free. Setting c5=4: `c6*A^4/(A^4+c7)`. Still not `A^2/(A^4+c)`.

Actually, let me reconsider. Can `A^2*c0 + A^c5*c6/(A^c5+c7)` combine to give `A^2/(c*A^4+1)`?

If c5=4: `c0*A^2 + c6*A^4/(A^4+c7)`. Common denominator: `(c0*A^2*(A^4+c7) + c6*A^4)/(A^4+c7)` = `(c0*A^6 + c0*c7*A^2 + c6*A^4)/(A^4+c7)`. GT rational part is `k*A^2/(c*A^4+1)`. For these to match, numerator must be proportional to A^2, requiring c0=0 (to kill A^6) and c6=0 (to kill A^4). Then we get 0. Not helpful.

If c5=2: `c0*A^2 + c6*A^2/(A^2+c7)` = `A^2*(c0*A^2 + c0*c7 + c6)/(A^2+c7)`. This is `A^2*(c0*A^2 + (c0*c7+c6))/(A^2+c7)`. GT needs `A^2/(c*A^4+1)`. Denominators don't match (A^2 vs A^4).

**Candidate 13:** `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A**c2*c3/(A**c2 + c4) + c5 + c6*exp(c7*t) + c8/A**5 + c9/A**5`

Setting c2=2, and trying: `c0*A^2 + c3*A^2/(A^2+c4)` — same problem, can't get A^4 denominator.

**Candidate 29:** Has both `A*c1/(A*c2+1)` and `A**c4*c5/(A**c4+c6)`. Setting c4=4: `c5*A^4/(A^4+c6)` plus other terms. Still can't produce `A^2/(A^4+1)`.
